### Equals(DataResource)

Determines whether the specified *other*  object is equal to the current instance of [DataResource](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-dataresource.html). This is an abstract declaration only. Derived classes must implement the correct Equals comparison for that class.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public bool Equals(DataResource other)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| other | DataResource | The DataResource object to compare with the current instance. |

#### Returns

true if *other*  is equal to the current instance of [DataResource](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-dataresource.html); otherwise false.

## TOPIC 00761: DataResource Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-data-dataresource.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-data-dataresource.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a source of data for a real-time sequence. Derives fromINotifyPropertyChangedICloneableIEquatable< DataResource >SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Datapublic class DataResource : INotifyPropertyChanged, ICloneable, IEquatable< DataResource >RemarksThis class is the base class

### DataResource Class

Represents a source of data for a real-time sequence.

#### Derives from

- INotifyPropertyChanged
- ICloneable
- IEquatable< DataResource >

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public class DataResource : INotifyPropertyChanged, ICloneable, IEquatable< DataResource >

#### Remarks

This class is the base class for [DataValue](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue.html) and [SystemDefinitionChannelResource](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-systemdefinitionchannelresource.html). The Stimulus Profile API represents each parameter assignment to a real-time sequence call as a DataResource.

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DataResource(DataResource) | Initializes a new instance of DataResource by copying an existing instance. |
| DataResource() | Initializes a new instance of DataResource. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Clone() | Creates a new object that is a copy of the current data resource. |
| Equals(DataResource) | Determines whether the specified other object is equal to the current instance of DataResource. This is an abstract declaration only. Derived classes must implement the correct Equals comparison for that class. |

#### Events

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PropertyChanged | Occurs when a property value changes. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data

## TOPIC 00766: Equals(DataResource)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue-equals__dataresource.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue-equals__dataresource.html

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns a value indicating whether this instance is equal to the specified DataResource object. This method uses Type and Units to determine equivalency. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Datapublic override bool Equals(DataResource other)ParametersNameTypeDescriptionotherDataResourceTh

### Equals(DataResource)

Returns a value indicating whether this instance is equal to the specified [DataResource](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-dataresource.html) object. This method uses [Type](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue-type.html) and [Units](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue-units.html) to determine equivalency.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public override bool Equals(DataResource other)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| other | DataResource | The data resource to compare to this instance. |

#### Returns

true if *other*  has the same type and units as this instance; otherwise false.

Parent topic:

DataValue Class

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=veristand-net-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00776: DataValue Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-data-datavalue.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents the value of data for a real-time sequence. Derives fromDataResourceSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Datapublic class DataValue : DataResourceRemarksThis class is a base class for all primitive data types available in real-time sequences. The Stimulus Profile API uses DataVa

### DataValue Class

Represents the value of data for a real-time sequence.

#### Derives from

- DataResource

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public class DataValue : DataResource

#### Remarks

This class is a base class for all primitive data types available in real-time sequences. The Stimulus Profile API uses DataValue where primitive data types are appropriate, but channel references are not, such as the return value of a real-time sequence.

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DataValue(string) | Initializes a new instance of DataValue with the specified units. |
| DataValue(DataValue) | Initializes a new instance of DataValue by copying an existing instance. |
| DataValue() | Initializes a new instance of DataValue. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Size | Gets the size of the data value. |
| Type | Gets the data type of the data value. |
| Units | Gets or sets the units of the data value. Units can be any string that makes sense for the data value. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Equals(DataResource) | Returns a value indicating whether this instance is equal to the specified DataResource object. This method uses Type and Units to determine equivalency. |
| Equals(object) | Returns a value indicating whether this instance is equal to the specified object, which must be a DataValue object. This method uses Body and the CaseValue to determine equivalency. |
| GetBytes() | Returns the data value as an array of bytes. |
| GetHashCode() | Serves as a hash function for a DataValue object. The hash code this method returns is suitable for use in hashing algorithms and data structures like a hash table. |
| SetBytes(byte[]) | Sets the DataValue based on Bytes . This is an abstract declaration only. Derived classes must implement the correct SetBytes method for that class. |
| GetDataValueOfType(DataType) | Returns a DataValue object with the specified data type. |
| ToBestInt(string) | Returns a DataValue object representing an I32Value, U32Value, I64Value, or U64Value. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data

| I32ValueArray(IEnumerable< int >) | Initializes a new instance of I32ValueArray with the specified list of int values. |
| I32ValueArray(I32Value[]) | Initializes a new instance of I32ValueArray with the specified array of I32Value objects. |
| I32ValueArray(I32ValueArray) | Initializes a new instance of I32ValueArray by copying an existing I32ValueArray instance. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Clone() | Creates a new object that is a copy of the current 32-bit signed value array. |

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-data-i64value.html`

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a 64-bit signed integer. Derives fromScalarDataValueSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Datapublic class I64Value : ScalarDataValueThread SafetyAny members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.ConstructorsNameDescriptionI64Value()Initializes a new instance of I64Va

### I64Value Class

Represents a 64-bit signed integer.

#### Derives from

- ScalarDataValue

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public class I64Value : ScalarDataValue

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| I64Value() | Initializes a new instance of I64Value. |
| I64Value(long) | Initializes a new instance of I64Value with the specified value. |
| I64Value(I64Value) | Initializes a new instance of I64Value by copying an existing I64Value instance. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Size | Gets the size of the 64-bit signed integer. |
| Type | Gets the data type of the 64-bit signed integer. |
| Value | Gets or sets the value of the 64-bit signed integer. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Clone() | Creates a new object that is a copy of the current 64-bit signed value. |
| CompareTo(ScalarDataValue) | Compares this instance to a specified object and returns an integer that indicates their relationship to each other. |
| Equals(DataResource) | Returns a value indicating whether this instance is equal to the specified DataResource object. |
| FromString(string) | Converts the specified string to its long equivalent. |
| GetBytes() | Returns the 64-bit signed integer as an array of bytes. |
| SetBytes(byte[]) | Sets the value of I64Value based on Bytes . |
| ToBoolean() | Returns if this instance is a nonzero value. |
| ToDouble() | Returns the value of this instance as a double-precision floating point number. |
| ToInt32() | Returns the value of this instance as an equivalent 32-bit signed integer. |
| ToInt64() | Returns the value of this instance as an equivalent 64-bit signed integer. |
| ToString() | Returns the value of this instance as an equivalent string. |
| ToUInt32() | Returns the value of this instance as an equivalent 32-bit unsigned integer. |
| ToUInt64() | Returns the value of this instance as an equivalent 64-bit unsigned integer. |

### ImportedDoubleValueArray(string, string, string, ulong, ulong)

Initializes a new instance of the [ImportedDoubleValueArray](nationalinstruments-veristand-data-importeddoublevaluearray.html) class with the specified import file and channel.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public ImportedDoubleValueArray(string filePath, string channelGroup, string channel, ulong importLength, ulong importOffset)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| filePath | string | The path of the file from which to import values. |
| channelGroup | string | The name of the group in the import file that owns the channel . |
| channel | string | The name of the channel in the import file that contains data you want to import. |
| importLength | ulong | The number of samples to import, starting at the importOffset of the first sample you want to import. |
| importOffset | ulong | The index of the first sample you want to import. |

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents an array of double-precision, floating point numbers imported from a file. Derives fromDataValueArray< T >SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Datapublic class ImportedDoubleValueArray : DataValueArray< T >RemarksThe imported array value is read-only, so the real-time sequence c

### ImportedDoubleValueArray Class

Represents an array of double-precision, floating point numbers imported from a file.

#### Derives from

- DataValueArray< T >

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data](nationalinstruments-veristand-data.html)

public class ImportedDoubleValueArray : DataValueArray< T >

#### Remarks

The imported array value is read-only, so the real-time sequence cannot change array values.

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ImportedDoubleValueArray(string, string, string, ulong, ulong) | Initializes a new instance of the ImportedDoubleValueArray class with the specified import file and channel. |
| ImportedDoubleValueArray() | Initializes a new instance of the ImportedDoubleValueArray class. |
| ImportedDoubleValueArray(ImportedDoubleValueArray) | Initializes a new instance of the ImportedDoubleValueArray class by copying an existing instance. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Channel | Gets or sets the name of the channel in the import file that contains data you want to import. |
| ChannelGroup | Gets or sets the name of the group in the import file that owns the Channel. |
| ChildType | Gets the data type of the elements in ImportedDoubleValueArray. |
| FilePath | Gets or sets the path of the file from which to import values. |
| ImportSubsetLength | Gets or sets a value that specifies how many samples to import, starting with the ImportSubsetStartValue. |
| ImportSubsetStartValue | Gets or sets the index of the first sample you want to import. |
| Length | Gets the total number of elements in ImportedDoubleValueArray. |
| Offset | Gets or sets the amount by which channel values are offset along the y-axis. |
| Scale | Gets or sets the multiplier by which channel values are scaled along the y-axis. |
| Size | Gets the size of the array. |
| Type | Gets the data type of the ImportedDoubleValueArray. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Clone() | Creates a new object that is a copy of the current imported double array value. |
| Equals(DataResource) |  |
| Equals(object) | Determines whether the specified obj , which must be a ImportedDoubleValueArray, is equal to the current ImportedDoubleValueArray. |
| GetBytes() | Returns the array of double-precision, floating point numbers as an array of bytes. |
| GetHashCode() | Serves as a hash function for a ImportedDoubleValueArray object. The hash code that this method returns is suitable for using in hashing algorithms and data structures such as hash tables. |
| GetValues() | Returns an array that contains a value for each element of ImportedDoubleValueArray. |
| SetBytes(byte[]) | Performs no operation. |
| ToString() | Returns a string representation of the channel name and channel group name. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Data

| --- | --- |

### Equals(AbstractDeclaration)

Determines whether the specified *other*  object is equal to the current instance of [AbstractDeclaration](nationalinstruments-veristand-realtimesequencedefinitionapi-abstractdeclaration.html). Equality is determined using the [DefaultValue](nationalinstruments-veristand-realtimesequencedefinitionapi-abstractdeclaration-defaultvalue.html) and [Identifier](nationalinstruments-veristand-realtimesequencedefinitionapi-abstractdeclaration-identifier.html).

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| other | AbstractDeclaration | The AbstractDeclaration object to compare with the current instance. |

#### Returns

true if the specified *other*  object is equal to the current instance. Otherwise, false.
